# What's New

Refer to the following tables to learn about the product or doc changes in TikTok API for Business. 

# 2026

## May, 2026
```xtable
| Date{15%} | Type of change{15%} | API category{15%} | Changes{55%} |
|---|---|---|---|
| May 22nd, 2026 | Product enhancement | Others | We have introduced two new response parameters, `template_name` and `supported_objectives`, to [/page/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/get-the-page-id/v1.3). With this enhancement, you can quickly identify the campaign objectives supported by a given page template and integrate instant pages into your ads with greater confidence and speed. |
| May 15th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Accounts | We have enhanced the [/business/video/list/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/get-post-data-of-a-tiktok-account/v1.3) endpoint by adding `is_ad` as a response parameter and as a supported field in the `fields` request parameter. This update allows you to determine if a post is currently being promoted as an ad. The added visibility streamlines the process of monitoring Spark Ads performance and selecting posts that can be authorized for advertising. |
| May 8th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have enhanced our Pulse ad groups by introducing support for the 6s view-through rate (View+) optimization goal. This is available in TikTok Pulse ad groups when `optimization_goal` is set to `REACH` and `cpv_video_duration` is set to `SIX_SECONDS` in the [/adgroup/rf/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/create-an-r&f-ad-group/v1.3) endpoint. Additionally, a new view-optimized delivery strategy is available through the enum value `VIEW_OPTIMIZE` for the `delivery_mode` parameter in the [/adgroup/rf/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/create-an-r&f-ad-group/v1.3), [/adgroup/rf/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/update-an-r&f-ad-group/v1.3), and [/adgroup/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/get-ad-groups/v1.3) endpoints, empowering you to maximize view-through rates and capture greater audience attention. |
```

## April, 2026
```xtable
| Date{15%} | Type of change{15%} | API category{15%} | Changes{55%} |
|---|---|---|---|
| April 24th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have expanded support for interaction add-ons to regular Upgraded Smart+ Web Campaigns and Upgraded Smart+ E-commerce Catalog Ads. You can now manage these add-ons using the `interactive_add_on_list` parameter in the [/smart_plus/ad/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/create-an-upgraded-smart-ad/v1.3) and [/smart_plus/ad/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/update-an-upgraded-smart-ad/v1.3) endpoints, helping you drive more engagement. Learn how to [create a regular Upgraded Smart+ Web Campaign](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/create-a-regular-upgraded-smart-web-campaign/v1.3) and [Upgraded Smart+ E-commerce Catalog Ads](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/create-upgraded-smart-e-commerce-catalog-ads/v1.3) with this feature. |
| April 24th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Reporting | We have enhanced our reporting capabilities by adding three new social metrics: `cost_per_consideration`, `new_consideration_rate`, and `new_consideration_size`. These metrics are now available in both [basic reports](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/basic-reports-supported-metrics/v1.3) and [Upgraded Smart+ Creative Overview Reports](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/supported-ad-level-metrics-for-upgraded-smart-creative-reports/v1.3), providing you with deeper insights into your consideration audience. |
| April 24th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Tools | We have expanded our keyword discovery capabilities by extending regional support for the [/tool/search_keyword/keyword_idea/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/discover-new-keywords/v1.3) endpoint in 11 additional regions. You can now research keyword ideas in more markets, such as the United Kingdom, France, and Canada, gaining greater insight into local search trends. |
| April 17th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have expanded age targeting options for Upgraded Smart+ App Install and App Retargeting campaigns. You can now target users aged 13-17 by using the new enum value `AGE_13_17` for the `age_groups` parameter and `ALL` for `spc_audience_age` across the [/smart_plus/adgroup/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/create-an-upgraded-smart-ad-group/v1.3), [/smart_plus/adgroup/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/update-an-upgraded-smart-ad-group/v1.3), and [/smart_plus/adgroup/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/get-upgraded-smart-ad-groups/v1.3) endpoints. |
| April 17th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have broadened support for retargeting custom audiences in Upgraded Smart+ campaigns, specifically for [Catalog Ads for App](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/create-upgraded-smart-catalog-ads-for-app/v1.3) and [E-commerce Catalog Ads](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/create-upgraded-smart-e-commerce-catalog-ads/v1.3). You can now leverage the parameters `shopping_ads_retargeting_type`, `shopping_ads_retargeting_actions_days`, `included_custom_actions`, `excluded_custom_actions`, and `shopping_ads_retargeting_custom_audience_relation` in the [/smart_plus/adgroup/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/create-an-upgraded-smart-ad-group/v1.3), [/smart_plus/adgroup/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/update-an-upgraded-smart-ad-group/v1.3), and [/smart_plus/adgroup/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/get-upgraded-smart-ad-groups/v1.3) endpoints to re-engage audiences based on specific behavior in these ads.|
| April 10th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have expanded tracking functionalities for Upgraded Smart+ App Install and App Retargeting campaigns by incorporating `tracking_pixel_id` and `tracking_offline_event_set_ids` to the [/smart_plus/ad/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/create-an-upgraded-smart-ad/v1.3), [/smart_plus/ad/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/update-an-upgraded-smart-ad/v1.3), and [/smart_plus/ad/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/get-upgraded-smart-ads/v1.3) endpoints. This enhancement helps you measure a full spectrum of user engagement, covering both online website activities like add-to-cart and offline events like in-store purchases. |
| April 3rd, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have enhanced Upgraded Smart+ Catalog Ads for Website and App Optimization by introducing custom audience retargeting. You can now leverage the new parameters `shopping_ads_retargeting_type`, `shopping_ads_retargeting_actions_days`, `included_custom_actions`, `excluded_custom_actions`, and `shopping_ads_retargeting_custom_audience_relation` in the [/smart_plus/adgroup/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/create-an-upgraded-smart-ad-group/v1.3), [/smart_plus/adgroup/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/update-an-upgraded-smart-ad-group/v1.3), and [/smart_plus/adgroup/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/get-upgraded-smart-ad-groups/v1.3) endpoints to re-engage audiences based on specific behavior. |
| April 3rd, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have introduced the [/campaign/gmv_max/creative/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/remove-or-add-back-creatives-in-a-gmv-max-campaign/v1.3) endpoint to streamline creative management for GMV Max Campaigns. You can now easily remove or add back creatives in your Product or Live GMV Max Campaigns, ensuring your advertising efforts remain agile and effective. |
| April 3rd, 2026 | Product enhancement | Reporting | We have expanded reporting capabilities for Product GMV Max Campaigns by adding two new dimension groups for creative-level metrics: `&#91;"campaign_id","item_group_id","item_id","stat_time_day"&#93;` and `&#91;"item_id","stat_time_day"&#93;`. These additions allow for more granular performance tracking and optimization. Learn more about [metrics in GMV Max Campaign reports](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs/metrics-in-gmv-max-campaign-reports/v1.3). |
| April 3rd, 2026 | Product enhancement | Developer Experience | We have updated our developer documentation links to be more semantic and descriptive. These new links are based on the document's title and content, making it easier for you to identify the information you will see at a glance. |
```

## March, 2026
```xtable
| Date{15%} | Type of change{15%} | API category{15%} | Changes{55%} |
|---|---|---|---|
| March 27th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have introduced new parameters `product_titles`, `product_image_list`, `catalog_tag_list`, `promo_info_list`, and `product_info_enabled` to the [/smart_plus/ad/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843317390059522), [/smart_plus/ad/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843317411665921), and [/smart_plus/ad/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843317378982914) endpoints. By incorporating product details and promo code or offer details into your Upgraded Smart+ Ads, you can leverage our system to generate tailored ad variations, ultimately improving ad performance and highlighting offers to drive user engagement. |
| March 27th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Reporting | We have enhanced synchronous audience reports by adding the [dimensions](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1751454103714818) `bucket_id` and `stat_time_hour`, along with the `cost` [metric](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1751454162042882). This allows you to group reporting data by Real-Time API bucket ID, empowering you to fine-tune your real-time bidding strategies based on the user characteristics of different buckets and assess various approaches across traffic segments. |
| March 20th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Reporting | We have enhanced our Basic reports with new TikTok metrics for deeper insights into user actions like purchases, ad revenue, and subscriptions. This update empowers you to track key performance indicators more effectively. For a detailed comparison, please see the "<b>Comparing v1.2 and v1.3</b>" section in [Basic reports > Supported metrics](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1751443967255553#item-link-Comparing%20v1.2%20and%20v1.3). |
| March 20th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Reporting | We have launched the [Reporting Subscription API](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1859914816615617), which allows you to monitor changes to reporting metrics like `spend`, `impressions`, `clicks`, and `video_play_actions`. This new tool provides minute-level notifications for your ad accounts, empowering faster, data-driven decisions. |
| March 20th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Business Center | We have rolled out several enhancements to streamline your management of Payment Portfolios. Key updates include adding the `payment_portfolio_id` parameter to [/bc/balance/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739939128198145) for balance retrieval and to [/bc/transfer/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739939095321601) for transfers, which now also details participant accounts through the response parameters `payee_account` and `remitter_account`. Furthermore, we added the `payment_portfolio_type` response field to key endpoints, including [/advertiser/balance/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739939106470913), [/payment_portfolio/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1839151986039809), and [/payment_portfolio/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1839151931301954), enabling clearer identification of Advanced and Standard Payment Portfolios.  |
| March 13th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have rolled out updates to give you better control over your Spark Ads Push content. You can now retrieve `ads_only_mode` and `username` from [/identity/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740218420781057) and the `username` from [/identity/info/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740218453385217). Furthermore, [/advertiser/info/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739593083610113) now supports `ads_only_mode` to help you verify the ad account’s mandatory "Show through ads only" mode status and prevent accidental profile posts from Spark Ads Push. |
| March 13th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have enhanced our Upgraded Smart+ E-commerce Catalog Ads capabilities. The Upgraded Smart+ Ads endpoints ([/smart_plus/ad/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843317390059522), [/smart_plus/ad/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843317411665921), and [/smart_plus/ad/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843317378982914)) now support `catalog_creative_info`, `identity_authorized_bc_id`, and new identity types `TT_USER` and `BC_AUTH_TT` for the parameter `identity_type` within `ad_configuration`. This allows you to leverage Spark Ads for catalog creatives with more flexible media settings. |
| March 13th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have enhanced the ad preview functionality for Upgraded Smart+ E-commerce Catalog Ads. The [/smart_plus/ad/preview/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843317445798914) endpoint now accepts `identity_authorized_bc_id` and `catalog_creative_info` parameters, along with the `TT_USER` and `BC_AUTH_TT` identity types. This enhancement allows you to accurately preview your E-commerce Catalog Ads using Spark Ads with more flexible media settings before launch. |
| March 6th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have expanded the maximum size of the `item_group_ids` request parameter from 50 to 400 for the [/campaign/gmv_max/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1822000988713089) and [/campaign/gmv_max/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1822001009002497) endpoints. This enhancement allows you to include significantly more products in a single Product GMV Max Campaign, streamlining your campaign management. |
| March 6th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have added the `quantity` parameter to the response of the [/store/product/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1793482248880130) endpoint. This new field provides the product count from your TikTok Shop, a useful metric for planning and executing Product GMV Max Campaigns. |
| March 6th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have added the `accelerate_testing_for_new_videos` parameter across our GMV Max Campaign API endpoints, including [/campaign/gmv_max/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1822000988713089), [/campaign/gmv_max/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1822001009002497), and [/campaign/gmv_max/info/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1822000968821762). This feature allows you to prioritize performance testing for new, recently authorized, and updated videos within your GMV Max Campaigns. |
| March 6th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have enhanced the ad account creation process via the [/bc/advertiser/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739939020318721) endpoint. It now accepts a `payment_info` request parameter and returns `payment_portfolio_binding_result` and `budget_setup_result`, allowing for simultaneous Payment Portfolio linking and budget configuration. |
| March 6th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have added the `amount_info` request parameter to the [/bc/transfer/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739939095321601) endpoint. This allows you to specify the exact cash, voucher, or credit amount to be processed at the ad account level, offering more precise fund transfers. |
```
## February, 2026
```xtable
| Date{15%} | Type of change{15%} | API category{15%} | Changes{55%} |
|---|---|---|---|
| February 27th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have expanded budget options for non-CBO campaigns within the Upgraded Smart+ API endpoints ([/smart_plus/campaign/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843312852800706), [/smart_plus/campaign/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843312876001282), [/smart_plus/campaign/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843312818332930)). You can now use the `BUDGET_MODE_DAY` and `BUDGET_MODE_TOTAL` enum values for the `budget_mode` parameter to define either a daily or a lifetime budget limit for all ad groups under a non-CBO campaign. This enhancement empowers you with greater precision in budget allocation, ensuring more efficient campaign spending. |
| February 13th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Accounts | We have enhanced our comment functionalities by introducing a new endpoint, [/business/comment/image/upload/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1856212334897154), for uploading images. Correspondingly, creating comments or replies with an image is now possible through new request parameters (`image_uri`, `image_width`, `image_height`) and a response parameter (`image_url`) in [/business/comment/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1762228442072066) and [/business/comment/reply/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1762228448779266). You can also retrieve images in comments and replies via the `image_url` response parameter in [/business/comment/list/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1760232109619202) and [/business/comment/reply/list/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1762228430145538). |
| February 13th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Business Messaging | We have added the `original_msg_id` parameter to the Business Messaging webhook events [im_send_msg](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1832190670631937#item-link-im_send_msg) and [im_receive_msg](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1832190670631937#item-link-im_receive_msg). This enhancement allows you to retrieve the ID of the message that received a reaction, enriching the contextual data available for reactions.|
| February 6th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have introduced the `disclaimer` parameter to the Upgraded Smart+ endpoints, including [/smart_plus/ad/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843317390059522), [/smart_plus/ad/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843317411665921), and [/smart_plus/ad/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843317378982914). This enhancement allows you to configure either text-only or clickable disclaimers for your Upgraded Smart+ Ads, ensuring compliance and clarity for your audience. |
| February 6th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have introduced the `creative_auto_add_toggle` parameter to the Upgraded Smart+ endpoints [/smart_plus/ad/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843317390059522), [/smart_plus/ad/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843317411665921), and [/smart_plus/ad/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843317378982914). This gives you the ability to control whether newly generated assets are automatically added to your ads during delivery, providing more precise management over your creative assets. |
| February 6th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have introduced the `creative_auto_enhancement_strategy_list` parameter across several endpoints, including Upgraded Smart+ endpoints ([/smart_plus/ad/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843317390059522), [/smart_plus/ad/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843317411665921), [/smart_plus/ad/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843317378982914)), Manual Ads endpoints ([/ad/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739953377508354), [/ad/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739953405142018), [/ad/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1735735588640770)), and the Campaign Copy endpoint [/campaign/copy/task/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1788434394151938). This feature provides a powerful way to optimize your ad creatives automatically. [Learn more about Automatic Enhancements](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1855450880142402). |
| February 6th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Tools | We have launched the new endpoint [/tool/search_keyword/keyword_idea/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1855460985594881). This tool empowers you to discover new keywords for your Search Ads Campaigns, helping you reach people interested in your business more effectively. |
```

## January, 2026
```xtable
| Date{15%} | Type of change{15%} | API category{15%} | Changes{55%} |
|---|---|---|---|
| January 30th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have enhanced the [/gmv_max/report/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1824721673497601) endpoint by adding the enum value `STATUS_ALL` to the `campaign_statuses` parameter. This feature enables you to fetch performance data across all your GMV Max Campaigns at once, providing a comprehensive overview of your advertising efforts. |
| January 30th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Generic | We have added the `ads_only_mode` response parameter to [/identity/info/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740218453385217). This new parameter helps you confirm whether an identity is restricted to creating ads in "Ads-only mode", giving you better control over ad-focused content delivery. |
| January 30th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Business Center | We have launched the new [/bc/oa/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1855027199571138) endpoint for creating Organization Accounts within a Direct or Agency Business Center. Additionally, the new `verification_status` response parameter in [/bc/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1737115687501826) lets you check a Business Center's verification status before creating accounts, ensuring a smoother setup process. For more details, see [Organization Account](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1855026897423361). |
| January 30th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Business Center | We have enhanced our Business Center functionalities for more streamlined TikTok account management. <ul><li>The [/bc/asset/advertiser/assign/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1846868953025538) endpoint now supports linking TikTok accounts for both advertising and organic purposes through the `asset_type` parameter. </li><li>To complement this, two new endpoints are now available: [/bc/asset/advertiser/unassign/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1855027260369921) to revoke the linkage of a TikTok account to an ad account, and [/bc/asset/advertiser/assigned/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1855027294743554) to retrieve the list of linked TikTok accounts. </li><li>For easier retrieval and management, the `MANAGED_BUSINESS_ACCOUNT` enum value has been added to the `asset_type` parameter in [/bc/asset/admin/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739433007779841), [/bc/asset/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739432717798401), and [/bc/asset/member/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739659558931458). These endpoints also return richer data with new response parameters including `business_account_roles`, `is_business_verified`, `operating_region_code`, `tt_asset_handle`, and `tt_asset_profile_image`. </li><li>Finally, permission workflows are simplified by adding the `MANAGED_BUSINESS_ACCOUNT` enum value to the `asset_type` parameter in [/bc/asset/assign/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739438211077121) and [/bc/asset/unassign/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739448126749698), with the former also gaining a new `business_account_roles` request parameter for more granular role assignment.</li></ul>|
| January 23rd, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have made the [Upgraded Smart+ API](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843301794874370) available, supporting an enhanced campaign structure with upgraded Smart+ experience built-in campaign management. This enhancement helps you create and manage campaigns more efficiently within a unified framework. Discover more about the [Upgraded Smart+ Campaign](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1853452461203458). |
| January 16th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Creatives | We have expanded our ad preview capabilities in [/creative/ads_preview/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739403070695426) by introducing support for CapCut and Lemon8 placements of Auction Reach ads. This update includes adding the enum value `PLACEMENT_GLOBAL_APP_BUNDLE` to the `placement` parameter, a new `tiktok_subplacement` parameter, and the enum value `IN_FEED_TWO_COLUMNS` for `preview_format`. |
| January 16th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Accounts | We have enhanced our content publishing capabilities by adding the `music_sound_info` parameter to [/business/video/publish/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1762228496095234) and [/business/photo/publish/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1803630424390658). You can now attach a track from the Commercial Music Library when you publish videos or photos. |
| January 16th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Discovery | We have added the `full_duration_song_clip` and `trending_song_clip` response parameters to the [/discovery/cml/trending_list/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1825119063013505) endpoint. This allows you to retrieve the most trending clip from a popular track. |
| January 9th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have enhanced our GMV Max Campaign management by adding the new parameters `promotion_days` and `auto_budget` to the [/campaign/gmv_max/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1822000988713089), [/campaign/gmv_max/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1822001009002497), and [/campaign/gmv_max/info/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1822000968821762) endpoints. This update allows you to enable automatic budget increase during promotion days and non-promotion days and customize the increase percentage and increase limit for better campaign performance. |
| January 9th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have enhanced the [/ad/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739953377508354) endpoint to support Zefr as a viewability partner. The enum value `ZEFR` has been added to the `viewability_postbid_partner` parameter, allowing you to enable Zefr for post-bid third-party viewability measurement on your Manual Ads. |
| January 9th, 2026 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We now support Inventory filter and Category exclusions for Search Ads Campaigns. You can enable these features through the `brand_safety_type` and `category_exclusion_ids` parameters using the [/adgroup/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739499616346114) endpoint. For more details on usage scenarios, refer to our guide on how to [Create Search Ads Campaigns](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1815394136739841). |
| January 9th, 2026 | Product enhancement | TikTok One | We have expanded the metrics for TikTok One Creator Marketplace reports in [/tto/tcm/report/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1815693573340162) to include `reach_organic`, `reach_paid`, `video_completion_rate_organic`, `video_completion_rate_paid`, `average_view_time_organic`, `average_view_time_paid`, `organic_two_seconds_views`, `paid_two_seconds_views`, `organic_six_seconds_views`, `paid_six_seconds_views`, and `audience_language_distribution`. This update provides deeper insights into your videos' reach, views, and audience language distribution. |
```
# 2025
## December, 2025
```xtable
| Date{15%} | Type of change{15%} | API category{15%} | Changes{55%} |
|---|---|---|---|
| December 26th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Generic | We have introduced the `return_advertiser_ids` request parameter to the [/oauth2/access_token/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739965703387137) endpoint. You can now request an access token without retrieving the complete list of associated advertiser accounts, which reduces response times and avoids timeouts for tokens with access to too many advertisers. |
| December 19th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Reporting | We have launched the new endpoint [/campaign_label/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1851286489283585) to retrieve campaign labels for an ad account. Furthermore, we’ve expanded filtering in synchronous [basic](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1751443975608321), [audience](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1751454172429314), and [DSA](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1751625296192514) reports by adding the filters `campaign_label_ids`, `campaign_label_names`, and `campaign_label_types`, which helps you refine your analytics by campaign labels. |
| December 19th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have enhanced brand safety controls for all Search Ads Campaigns by supporting TikTok inventory filtering via the `brand_safety_type` parameter. Additionally, you can now enable category exclusions for Search Ads Campaigns under the Traffic and Lead Generation objectives using `category_exclusion_ids`, ensuring your ads appear alongside suitable content. For more details, see [Create Search Ads Campaigns](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1815394136739841). |
| December 19th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Accounts | We have enhanced the [/business/video/list/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1762228421622786) endpoint by adding the `media_type` response parameter. This feature provides a clear way to identify and differentiate between video posts and photo or text posts, streamlining content management. |
| December 12th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Reporting | We have enhanced our Basic reports to include new TikTok metrics, providing deeper insights into user actions such as purchases, checkouts, and ad impressions. To learn more about these new metrics, refer to the "<b>Comparing v1.2 and v1.3</b>" section in [Basic reports > Supported metrics](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1751443967255553#item-link-Comparing%20v1.2%20and%20v1.3).  |
| December 12th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Events | We have introduced the `automatic_advanced_matching_fields`, `enable_first_party_cookies`, and `enable_expanded_data_sharing` parameters to the [/pixel/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740858779758593), [/pixel/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740858799524865), and [/pixel/list/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740858697598978) endpoints. This allows for more granular control over Automatic Advanced Matching, first-party cookies, and expanded data sharing settings for your pixels, which will improve attribution and performance. |
| December 5th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Tools | We have enhanced the [/tool/search_keyword/recommend/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1838630375757825) endpoint by adding the `ad_ids` and `landing_page_urls` request parameters. This update enables you to retrieve recommended search keywords based on ad IDs or landing page URLs, helping you discover additional keywords and improve creative relevance. |
| December 5th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Others | We have added the `is_gpppa` response parameter to the [/identity/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740218420781057) and [/identity/info/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740218453385217) endpoints. This new parameter helps you identify if a TikTok account is a [Government, Politician, and Political Party Account](https://support.tiktok.com/en/using-tiktok/growing-your-audience/government-politician-and-political-party-accounts), enabling you to exclude these accounts from Spark Ads creation. |
```

| Date{15%} | Type of change{15%} | API category{15%} | Changes{55%} |

| November 28th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Business Messaging | We’ve enhanced our Business Messaging capabilities to support a wider range of interactive content. You can now retrieve sticker, emoji, and video messages, along with message reactions, using the [/business/message/content/list/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1832184425841170) endpoint, which includes the new `reactions`, `sticker`, `emoji`, and `video` response parameters and additional enum values `VIDEO`, `EMOJI`, and `STICKER` for the `message_type` parameter. Furthermore, video messages can be downloaded via the [/business/message/media/download/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1832184455450626) endpoint, and the [Webhook event `im_send_msg`](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1832190670631937#item-link-im_send_msg) now delivers detailed information for these new message types and reactions, including the new `reactions`, `sticker`, `emoji`, and `video` response parameters and additional enum values `video`, `emoji`, `sticker`, and `reaction` for the `message_type` parameter.  |
| November 28th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Business Center | We have enhanced the invoice creation process by adding the `campaign_id` request parameter to the [/bc/invoice/task/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1754000448122882) endpoint. This new feature allows you to filter invoices by a specific campaign, empowering you to conduct more granular financial analysis and reporting at the campaign level.|
| November 28th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have introduced an automatic budget increase feature for Smart+ Campaigns, now available in the [/campaign/spc/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1767334204047362), [/campaign/spc/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1767334250066945), and [/campaign/spc/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1767334299811842) endpoints. You can now use the `budget_auto_adjust_strategy` parameter to enable automatic budget increases when CPA, Day 0 ROAS, and budget targets are met, and retrieve the latest budget with `current_budget`, helping you maximize performance with less manual effort. |
| November 21st, 2025 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have expanded our campaign management capabilities to support Carousel Ads with the `REACH` objective. You can now create or preview these ads by utilizing the `ad_format` parameter in the [/ad/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739953377508354) and [/creative/ads_preview/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739403070695426) endpoints. | November 14th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Reporting |We have enhanced our reporting capabilities by introducing new metrics for LIVE GMV Max Campaigns. | November 14th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Business Center | We have enhanced our Business Center capabilities to provide more efficient management of TikTok account ad delivery permissions. You can now generate an authorization URL for ad delivery permissions using [/bc/asset/account/authorization/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1846868897541122) and link a TikTok account to an ad account in a Business Center with [/bc/asset/advertiser/assign/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1846868953025538). |
| November 14th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Tools | We have launched a health diagnosis tool for Search Ads Campaigns. This tool, available through the [/tool/diagnosis/search/health/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1848591212970082) endpoint, provides you with actionable insights on search volume and keyword relevance, along with bid and budget suggestions to enhance your campaign's effectiveness.|
| November 14th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Catalog Management | We have made several enhancements to the catalog products endpoints ([/catalog/product/upload/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740497429681153), [/catalog/product/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740562287852546), [/catalog/product/file/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740496787164161), and [/catalog/product/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740564136678402)) for hotel catalogs, including:<ul><li>Removing the parameters `phone`, `cancellation_policy`, `hotel_room_id`, `meal_policy`, `amenities`, and `total_price`.</li><li>Adding the parameters `secondary_address`, `tertiary_address`, `postal_code`, `internal_label_0`, and `internal_label_1`.</li><li>Changing the data type of the `hotel_category` and `room_type` parameters to string array.</li><li>Changing the values for the `hotel_category`, `loyalty_program`, and `room_type` parameters to enum values.</li><li>Increasing the max size for `additional_image_urls` from 10 to 20.</li><li>Decreasing the max size for `guest_ratings` from 5 to 1.</li><li>Changing the parameters `description`, `availability`, and `region` from required to optional for product uploads.</li></ul> Additionally, we have supported [Alias fields for hotel catalogs in CSV templates](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740496787164161#item-link-Alias%20fields%20for%20hotel%20catalogs).<br> These changes streamline your catalog setup and enhance integration with other platforms.|
| November 7th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have enhanced our campaign capabilities to include Website and App Optimization for [Manual Catalog Ads](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1839882947475458) and [Manual Non-Catalog Ads](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1839882969587906), allowing you to consolidate your advertising efforts across both website and app audiences. To implement this, use the new enum value `WEB_AND_APP` for the `sales_destination` parameter in campaign endpoints ([/campaign/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739318962329602), [/campaign/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739320422086657), [/campaign/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739315828649986)) and specify the `app_config` parameter in the ad group endpoints ([/adgroup/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739499616346114), [/adgroup/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739586761631745), and [/adgroup/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739314558673922)).|

| October 17th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Catalog Management | We have streamlined the entertainment catalog product setup in the catalog product endpoints ([/catalog/product/upload/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740497429681153), [/catalog/product/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740562287852546), [/catalog/product/file/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740496787164161), and [/catalog/product/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740564136678402)) by removing the parameters `availability`, `product_detail`, `product_detail.condition`,`star_rating`, `timeline`, and `category`. Additionally, we have increased the `additional_image_urls` size limit to 20 and made `landing_page_url` optional to enhance your workflow. | October 17th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Catalog Management | We have updated the [/catalog/product/upload/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740497429681153) and [/catalog/product/file/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740496787164161) endpoints to no longer require `landing_page` and `landing_page_url` for hotel, flight, and destination catalogs. This enhancement provides greater flexibility when setting up your travel-related products. |
| October 17th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Catalog Management | We have enhanced the catalog product endpoints ([/catalog/product/upload/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740497429681153), [/catalog/product/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740562287852546), [/catalog/product/file/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740496787164161), and [/catalog/product/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740564136678402)) for Auto-Inventory vehicles with new fields. These additions, including `offer_type`, `term_length`, `offer_term_qualifier`, `amount_price`, `amount_percentage`, `amount_qualifier`, `downpayment`, `downpayment_qualifier`, `offer_disclaimer`, `offer_disclaimer_url`, `emission_disclaimer`, `emission_disclaimer_url`, `emission_overlay_disclaimer`, and `emission_image_link`, enable you to provide comprehensive vehicle information, which boosts credibility and reinforces regulatory compliance. |
| October 17th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Accounts | We have introduced a required `secret` parameter to all URL properties endpoints ([/business/property/add/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1769325280876545), [/business/property/verify/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1769325308162050), [/business/property/delete/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1769325351919617), and [/business/property/list/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1769325368603650)), starting October 15th, 2025. This security measure is designed to prevent unauthorized postings to your TikTok account by restricting activity to verified domains and URL prefixes. |
| October 10th, 2025 | Product enhancement  | Business Messaging  | We have launched two new endpoints [/business/message/direct_reply/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843697551083522) and [/business/message/direct_reply/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1843697576682497) for managing the Comment-to-Message feature for Business Accounts. This feature enables businesses to proactively engage with users by sending direct messages in response to high-intent comments on their video posts. |
| October 10th, 2025 | Product enhancement  | Business Messaging  | We have introduced the [new webhook event `im_receive_high_intent_comment`](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1832190670631937#item-link-im_receive_high_intent_comment), which helps you identify high-intent comments on your video in real-time. Furthermore, the new `direct_reply` request parameter in [/business/message/send/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1832184403754242) allows you to send a direct reply to a comment on a video. |

## August, 2025
```xtable
| Date{15%} | Type of change{15%} | API category{15%} | Changes{55%} |
|---|---|---|---|
| August 29th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have expanded the value range for the request parameter `default_spark_ads_requested_authorization_days` in [/tto/tcm/campaign/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1815693549459458) to allow values from 0 to 365. Additionally, in [/tcm/tt_video/apply/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1751098904942594) the request parameter `authorization_days` now accepts values from 1 to 365, and a new request parameter `action` is introduced. These updates grant you enhanced flexibility in managing your campaigns and help streamline your advertising schedules.|
| August 29th, 2025 | Product enhancement | TikTok One  | We have introduced the response parameters `country_codes` and `failed_handle_names` to the endpoints [/tto/tcm/campaign/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1815693549459458) and [/tto/tcm/campaign/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1830338948169794). With these updates, you can effectively monitor uninvited creators and gain insights into the regions of your invited creators, improving your campaign strategies. |
| August 15th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have introduced the functionality to retrieve cost, `cost_per_order`, and `roi` metrics at the product and creative levels in our Product GMV Max Campaign reports. These additions empower you to evaluate the performance and impact of each product and creative. To learn about all available metrics, see [Metrics in GMV Max Campaign reports](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1824722485971009). |
| August 8th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management| We have added the enum value `ZEFR` to the response parameter `viewability_postbid_partner` in the endpoints [/ad/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739953405142018) and [/ad/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1735735588640770). | April 25th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Creative Management | We have expanded our interactive capabilities by introducing the Gesture add-on, accessible through the `GESTURE` enum value for the parameter `creative_portfolio_type` and the new parameters `gesture_type`,`slide_length`,`slide_dimension`, and `interactive_music_id` in ([/creative/portfolio/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739091950439426), [/creative/portfolio/get/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739092113671170), and [/creative/portfolio/list/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1766324010279938). For a step-by-step guide on how to use a Gesture in your ad, see [Premium Add-ons](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1749019676181505). |
| April 25th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Creative Management | We have streamlined the Smart Fix functionalities by limiting auto fixes to video resolution and size issues, providing a single fixed video. The [/business/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1762228399168514) endpoint now includes `unique_video_views`, `phone_number_clicks`, `lead_submissions`, `app_download_clicks`, `bio_link_clicks`, `email_clicks`, `address_clicks`, `daily_total_followers`, `daily_lost_followers`, `audience_ages`, `audience_cities`, and `engaged_audience`. Additionally, the [/business/video/list/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1762228421622786) endpoint offers `favorites`, `profile_views`, `website_clicks`, `phone_number_clicks`, `lead_submissions`, `app_download_clicks`, `email_clicks`, `address_clicks`, `video_view_retention`, `audience_genders`, `audience_cities`, `audience_types`, `new_followers`, and `engagement_likes`. These comprehensive metrics enable deeper insights into audience behavior and content performance. |
| January 24th, 2025 | Doc enhancement | Campaign Management | We have rebranded "Search Ads Toggle" to "[Automatic Search Placement](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1771747626094593)". |
| January 17th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have introduced two secondary status enum values `ADGROUP_STATUS_REVIEW_PARTIALLY_APPROVED` and `AD_STATUS_REVIEW_PARTIALLY_APPROVED`, giving you more granular visibility into partially rejected ad groups and ads. To learn more about secondary statuses, see [Supported secondary statuses for a primary status](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1757239620352002). |
| January 17th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Business Center | We have implemented support for multiple document types in UnionPay verification submissions through the new `representative_document_type` request parameter in [/bc/advertiser/unionpay_info/submit/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1813772274039809). This addition simplifies the verification process for China Outbound (CNOB) advertisers by accommodating various official documents, including passports. |
| January 10th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Creative Management | We have launched the TikTok Instant Page Editor SDK, allowing you to create Customized Pages, Instant Forms, App Profile Pages, and Pop-up Forms through a more streamlined page creation workflow. To learn about how to use the SDK, see [Instant Page Editor SDK](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740307202170881). |
| January 10th, 2025 | Product enhancement | Business Center | We have launched the endpoint [/changelog/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1820767460168705), allowing you to retrieve the activity log of your Business Center. This addition enables monitoring of changes and updates within your Business Center, enhancing your ability to manage business operations effectively. |
| January 3rd, 2025 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have enhanced the [/creative/cta/recommend/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739362202742785) endpoint with new request parameters, including `new_version`, `objective_type`, `promotion_type`,language, `app_id`, `placements`, `region_codes`, `optimization_goal`, `ad_texts`, and `landing_page_url`. These parameters enable dynamic CTA recommendations based on your specific ad configurations, allowing for more contextual CTA suggestions. To learn more about how to use the new parameters, see [Dynamic CTAs](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740307296329730#item-link-Dynamic%20CTAs). |

The hour-level latency window has been adjusted to 16 hours. Additionally, we've added detailed latency clarifications for more dimensions, helping you better plan your data analytics workflows. |
| December 20th, 2024 | Product enhancement | Accounts | We have added the response parameter `display_name` to [/business/comment/list/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1760232109619202) and [/business/comment/reply/list/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1762228430145538), enabling identification of commenters via display names in both primary comments and replies. | December 20th, 2024 | Product enhancement | Accounts | We have enhanced video publishing capabilities with the new `upload_to_draft` request parameter in [/business/video/publish/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1762228496095234) for draft uploads, and `SEND_TO_USER_INBOX` status in [/business/publish/status/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1816387106635778) for draft monitoring. ## August, 2024

```xtable
| Date{15%} | Type of change{15%} | API category{15%} | Changes{55%} |

This enhancement allows for more extensive location targeting in ad groups. |
| August 30th, 2024 | Product enhancement | Creative Management | We have extended the validity period of `preview_link` for `ADS_CREATION` and `AD` preview types in [/creative/ads_preview/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739403070695426) to 30 days, offering greater flexibility in the creative review process. |
| August 30th, 2024 | Doc enhancement | Campaign Management | We have introduced a use case topic [Create Community Interaction ads](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1808164002093058) to guide you through the steps of creating Community Interaction ads. |
| August 23rd, 2024 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management |We have expanded geographic targeting to 17 new countries or regions via `location_ids` in [/adgroup/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739499616346114) for `TRAFFIC`, `LEAD_GENERATION`, `APP_PROMOTION`, and `WEB_CONVERSIONS` objectives. Newly available locations include Azerbaijan, Bulgaria, Bolivia, Cyprus, Algeria, Estonia, Croatia, Kenya, Sri Lanka, Lithuania, Latvia, Nigeria, Puerto Rico, Paraguay, Serbia, Slovenia, Slovakia. To see the countries or regions that you can target, use [/tool/targeting/search/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1761236883355649) or [/tool/region/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1737189539571713).|

To check the campaign and ad group quota for an iOS app, use [/campaign/quota/info/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1752256376677378).|
| April 26th, 2024 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management |We have added the response parameter `advanced_dedicated_campaign_allowed` to [/app/list/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740859313270786) and [/app/info/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740859272887297) for querying an iOS app's eligibility for [Advanced Dedicated Campaigns](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1797011827608577) (ADCs). Additionally, we have added the parameter is_advanced_dedicated_campaign to Campaign API ([/campaign/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739318962329602), [/campaign/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739320422086657), [/campaign/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739315828649986), and [/campaign/copy/task/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1788434394151938)) and Smart Performance Campaign (SPC) API ([/campaign/spc/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1767334204047362), [/campaign/spc/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1767334250066945), and [/campaign/spc/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1767334299811842)) for creating Standard ADCs and SPC ADCs.|
| April 19th, 2024 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have launched the endpoint [/targeting/search/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1796638342793218) for searching for or listing targeting categories and hashtags related to interests and behaviors. Additionally, we have added the request parameter `language` to [/tool/region/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1737189539571713) for retrieving translated location names.|
| April 12th, 2024 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have supported `engaged_view_attribution_window` in [regular ad groups](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739499616346114) and [Smart Performance ad groups](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1767334204047362) for measuring conversions after someone watches at least six seconds of your video ads. To learn about the supported engaged view-through window options for different advertising objectives, see [Attribution window and event count](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1777694366654465). |
| April 12th, 2024 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have made `EXPANDED_INVENTORY`, `category_exclusion_ids`, and `vertical_sensitivity_id` generally available. To learn about these brand safety features, see [Brand safety](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739381752981505). |
| April 12th, 2024 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have enhanced the fallback mechanism of additional images in [Carousel Video Shopping Ads](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1766217791987713#item-link-Steps%20for%20creating%20VSA%20Carousel%20Ads). When you use `carousel_image_index` in such ads via [/ad/create/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739953377508354) or [/ad/update/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1739953405142018), products with available additional images will be delivered when there are two or more such products. In cases where there are fewer than two products with available additional images, all products will be delivered with their main images. |
| April 12th, 2024 | Product enhancement | Business Center | We have added the rules for ad account budget updates. For more information, see [Manage the balance allocation of Business Centers](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1781992772171778). |
| April 12th, 2024 | Product enhancement | Ad Measurement | We have added the response parameters `browser_event_total_count` and `server_event_total_count` to [/pixel/event/stats/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740858904557570) for retrieving the browser and server breakdown data for different pixel events set up for a pixel. Additionally, we have added the response parameter `ownership_status` to [/pixel/list/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1740858697598978) for determining if a pixel is owned by an advertiser. |
| April 12th, 2024 | Doc enhancement | General | We have added a new [Need Support](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1795190020378625) page, making it easier for you to find support information. |

|February 8th, 2024 | Product enhancement | Generic |We have implemented enhanced parameter handling rules to improve consistency and security across our API endpoints. Using non-compliant locations for parameters, such as including them in the query string for POST endpoints, may result in errors being returned. <ul><li> For GET endpoints, request parameters (excluding headers) should be exclusively included in the query string.</li><li>For POST endpoints, request parameters (excluding headers) should be included solely in the request body.</li></ul>|

| December 15th, 2023 | Product enhancement | Others | We have launched the [/identity/live/get/](https://business-api.tiktok.com/portal/docs?id=1785238052792321) endpoint for getting live videos under an identity.  |

| December 1st, 2023 | Product enhancement | Reporting | We have added new dimensions and metrics to basic reports and audience reports. <br>New dimensions in basic reports: `event_source_id`, `page_id`, `component_name`, `room_id`<br>New metrics in basic reports: `advertiser_id`, `advertiser_name`, `adgroup_download_url`, `profile_image`, `bid_secondary_goal`, `ad_id`, `ad_profile_image`, `ad_url`, `unique_ad_impression_events`, `cost_per_unique_ad_impression_event`, `customized_ad_impression_event_rate`, `ads_impression_events`, `cost_pre_ad_impression_event`, `value_per_ad_impression_event`, `total_ad_impression_events_value`, `total_ad_impression_roas`, `page_content_view_events`, `total_page_view_content_events_value`, `cost_per_page_content_view_event`, `page_content_view_event_rate`, `value_per_page_content_view_event`<br>New dimensions in audience reports: `ad_type`<br>New metrics in audience reports: `advertiser_id`, `advertiser_name`,  `app_promotion_type`, `adgroup_download_url`, `profile_image`, `bid_secondary_goal`, `ad_id`, `ad_profile_image`, `ad_url` |

|July 14th, 2023|Product enhancement|Reporting|We have supported four impression-based CVR metrics: `conversion_rate_v2`(in [basic](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1751443967255553), [audience](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1751454162042882), [playable ad](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1751617882108929), and [DSA](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1751625293044737) reports), `real_time_conversion_rate_v2`(in basic, and audience reports), `skan_conversion_rate_v2` and `skan_click_time_conversion_rate_v2` (both in basic reports).|
|July 14th, 2023|Product enhancement|Catalog Management|We have launched the endpoints [/diagnostic/catalog/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1771117232728066), [/diagnostic/catalog/product/task/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1771117279175682), and [/diagnostic/catalog/product/task/get/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1771117294731266) for obtaining catalog diagnostic information. To learn more about how to use Catalog Diagnostics, refer to [Create catalogs and add products - Obtain Catalog Diagnostics](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1754263112945665#item-link-Obtain%20Catalog%20Diagnostics).|
|July 14th, 2023|Product enhancement|Creative Management|We've added new fields (`is_smart_performance_campaign` and `image_ids`) and enum values (`APP_PROMOTION`, `WEB_CONVERSIONS` for the field `objective_type`, and `CAROUSEL_ADS` for the field `ad_format`) to the `ADS_CREATION` ad preview functionality in  [/creative/ads_preview/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739403070695426), bringing it in line with ad creation parameters and enabling previewing of non-VSA Carousel Ads, and ads with the objective App Promotion or Web Conversions.|
|July 14th, 2023|Product enhancement|Leads|We have updated the base URL or header for accessing leads data in EEA/CH/UK. See [/page/lead/task/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739052936772610) and [/page/lead/task/download/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739053563877378) to find out the paths for accessing leads data in different countries or regions. |
|July 14th, 2023|Product enhancement|Audience|We have deprecated the enum value `first_normal` in [Enumeration-Encryption Type](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?rid=7xusz43oh3h&id=1737174886619138#item-link-Encryption%20Type). |
|July 14th, 2023|Product enhancement|Reporting|We have improved validation logic and updated [FAQs](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1738864850353154) to inform you that if the `service_type` in the request does not match your advertiser account type, the report will return a 200 success code but an empty data list ([]). |
|July 14th, 2023|Product enhancement|Reporting|Starting from Jul 6,  we have changed the names of the following metrics in async reports. Specifically, the changes include renaming Clicks to Clicks (Destination), CPC to CPC (Destination), CTR to CTR (Destination), Total Engagement to Clicks (All) and Engagement Rate to CTR (All). Note that these updates will only change the column names for async reports and sync reports will not be affected.   |
|July 7th, 2023|Product enhancement|Reporting|We have added a new dimension `skan_postback_sequence` to [basic reports](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1751443956638721) for retrieving SKAN metric data breakdown by SKAN Postback Sequence.|
|July 7th, 2023|Doc enhancement|Generic|We have changed the topic name "Terminology" into "[Concepts](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?rid=7xusz43oh3h&id=1738928364967937)" and added definitions of some common concepts to help developers who are new to our API documentation know about concepts frequently occurring on our website. |
|July 3rd, 2023|Product enhancement|Creator Marketplace|We have launched two Authentication 2.0 endpoints [/tt_user/oauth2/token/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1768493902119937#item-link-Get%20an%20access%20token) and [/tt_user/oauth2/refresh_token/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1768493902119937#item-link-Renew%20an%20access%20token) for getting or renewing an access token respectively.  To learn about how to use these two endpoints, refer to [Get authorization from creators (New)](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1768506960432130).|
|July 3rd, 2023|Doc enhancement|Creator Marketplace|We have added the validation rules for <strong>TikTok account holder redirect URL v2</strong> in [Get authorization from creators (New) - Step 1: Share authorization URL with creator](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1768506960432130#item-link-Step%201%3A%20Share%20authorization%20URL%20with%20creator).|

| Date{15%} | Type of change{15%} | API category{15%} | Changes{55%} |

Additionally, a new [filter](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1751443975608321) `image_mode` is now available. |

| May 15th, 2023 | Product enhancement | Accounts | We have launched the new endpoint [/tt_user/token_info/get/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1765927978092545) for getting TikTok Account permission scopes authorized by the TikTok account user via access token. |
| May 15th, 2023 | Product enhancement | Creator Marketplace | We have launched the new endpoint [/tt_user/token_info/get/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1765926674648065) for getting TikTok Account permission scopes authorized by a creator on TikTok Creator Marketplace via access token. |
| May 12th, 2023 | Product enhancement | Campaign Management | We have added the parameter `tracking_offline_event_set_ids` to support tracking track and measure offline activity from people that see or interact with your ads via Ad endpoints ([/ad/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739953377508354), [/ad/update/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739953405142018), [/ad/get/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1735735588640770)) and ACO endpoints ([/ad/aco/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739473063234626), [/ad/aco/update/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739473077112833), [/ad/aco/get/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739473020978177)). |
| May 12th, 2023 | Product enhancement | Ad Measurement | We have launched new Offline Events endpoints [/offline/update/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1765596741157889), [/offline/delete/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1765596790860802), and [/offline/get/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1765596808589313) for managing Offline Event sets. To learn about how to manage Offline Event sets, see [Get Started](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1758051319816193). |
| May 12th, 2023 | Product enhancement | Creative Management | We have added the request parameters `report_type`, `material_ids`, `video_ids`, `start_time`, `end_time`, and `lifetime` to [/report/video_performance/get/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1738825259075586) for running a Video Insights report on a video and for setting the data time range. Also, key frame metrics `clicks`, `conversions`, `drop_off`, `retain`, `ctr`, and `cvr` are supported in a Video Insights report. To learn about Video Insights, see [Creative insights-Video Insights data](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1749023065231362). |
| May 8th, 2023 | Product enhancement | Creator Marketplace | We have added to [/tcm/report/get/v2/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1752366000747522) the metrics `engagement_rate_benchmark_p25`, `engagement_rate_benchmark_p50`, `video_complete_rate_benchmark_p25`, `video_complete_rate_benchmark_p50`, `video_view_retention`, `most_popular_country_state_distribution` , and `audience_interest_distribution` for getting insights into the benchmarks of engagement rate and video completion rate, video duration rate, the distribution of state-level locales, and the distribution of audience interests. |
| May 8th, 2023 | Product enhancement |Accounts | We have added to [/business/comment/list/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1760232109619202) the request parameters `comment_ids` and `include_replies` for specifying the comments to get details of and whether to include replies to the top-level comments respectively, and the response parameters `parent_comment_id` and `reply_list` that return comment ID and details of comment replies. |

## February, 2023
 ```xtable
| Date{15%} | Type of change{15%} | API category{15%} | Changes{55%} |
|---|---|---|
|February 24th, 2023 |Product enhancement|Campaign Management| We have supported creating a Lead Generation ad with a <strong>Website Form</strong> via a new parameter `promotion_target_type` in [/v1.3/adgroup/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739499616346114). For details, see [Create Lead Generation ads - Create a Lead Generation ad with a Website Form](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739470742024193).
|February 24th, 2023 |Product enhancement|Campaign Management| We have added the filter parameter `promotion_type` to the request of [/v1.3/adgroup/get/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739314558673922) for filtering promotion types.
|February 24th, 2023 |Product enhancement|Campaign Management| We have now supported new scenarios of `APP_PROMOTION`, `PRODUCT_SALES` and `ENGAGEMENT` in the `tracking_pixel_id` field via [/v1.3/ad/aco/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739473063234626), [/v1.3/ad/aco/update/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739473077112833), [/v1.3/ad/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739953377508354) and [/v1.3/ad/update/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739953405142018).
|February 24th, 2023 |Product enhancement|Audience Management| We have launched two new endpoints related to <strong>audience application</strong>. You can use [/v1.3/dmp/custom_audience/apply/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1758615097524225) to apply or disconnect a Custom Audience from multiple ad groups at the same time. You can use [/v1.3/dmp/custom_audience/apply/log/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1758615737388033) to get the latest application log for Custom Audience. 
|February 24th, 2023 |Product enhancement|Audience Management| We have launched a new endpoint [/v1.3/dmp/custom_audience/lookalike/update/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1758616888158209) to enable you to manually update a Lookalike Audience. 
|February 24th, 2023 |Product enhancement|Audience Management|We have added a new response parameter `is_creator` in [/v1.3/dmp/custom_audience/list/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739940506015746) and [/v1.3/dmp/custom_audience/get/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739940507792385). You can use this field and `shared` field to check audience ownership and shared status. Moreover, a new response parameter `create_time` has been added to [/v1.3/dmp/custom_audience/get/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739940507792385) to indicate the time when the audience was created. 
|February 24th, 2023 |Product enhancement|Audience Management| We have added two request parameters `product_source` and `promotion_type` in [/v1.3/ad/audience_size/estimate/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1740302379236353) to enable more granular audience estimation for Product Sales scenarios.
|February 24th, 2023 |Product enhancement|Reporting|We have added the new metric type <strong>Offline Event Metrics</strong> to Basic reports. For details, see [Basic report - Supported metrics](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1751443967255553).
|February 24th, 2023 |Product enhancement|Creative Management| We have supported creating a Product Card portfolio via the enum value `PRODUCT_CARD` for the parameter `creative_portfolio_type` and 18 new parameters in the request of [/v1.3/creative/portfolio/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?rid=wtljluwz8r&id=1739091950439426), and supported getting the details of Product Card portfolios via the enum value `PRODUCT_CARD` for the parameter `creative_portfolio_type` and new parameters `card_show_price`, `card_tags`, and `card_image_index` in the response of [/v1.3/creative/portfolio/get/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739092113671170).

|February 10th, 2023 |Product enhancement|Campaign Management|We have added the request parameter `share_disabled` to [/adgroup/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739499616346114) to allow disabling the sharing of ads in auction ad groups to third-party platforms. Previously, the feature was only available for Reach & Frequency ad groups.
|February 3rd, 2023 |Product enhancement|Campaign management |The ability to pin comments is no longer available in the TikTok app. To improve the app experience and create a safe community for our users, we are removing the pinning comments functionality through the API. The [/comment/pin/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1738957749292033&rid=sxdhaaz882k) and [/comment/pinned/get/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1738957797483522&rid=sxdhaaz882k) endpoints are now marked as <strong>deprecated</strong>. Please review your integration and make any necessary adjustments. 
|February 3rd, 2023 |Product enhancement |Audience management |We have added a new enum value `MULTIPLE_TYPES` to the `calculate_type` field to support uploading a file with multiple IDs in [/v1.3/dmp/custom_audience/file/upload/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739940567842818&rid=ghrv306q4rj). See [Create Customer File Audiences-File API](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1747012327159809&rid=w8dfmqpyld9) for detailed steps and sample files. 
|February 3rd, 2023 |Product enhancement  |Audience management  |We have increased the maximum file upload size from 50MB to <strong>250MB</strong> in [/v1.3/dmp/custom_audience/file/upload/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739940567842818&rid=ghrv306q4rj) to enable you to upload a larger file.

|December 2nd, 2022| Product enhancement |Campaign Management| We have deprecated BuzzVideo and Babe (`PLACEMENT_TOPBUZZ`) placements.  You can no longer place ads on BuzzVideo and Babe, and existing campaigns with `PLACEMENT_TOPBUZZ` placement will not be placed on BuzzVideo and Babe anymore. Moreover, if you update the existing adgroups which select `PLACEMENT_TOPBUZZ` as the only placement AND include `JP` or `TW` as locations,  an error will occur.  For details, see [Placements](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1745292441739265).
|December 2nd, 2022| Doc enhancement |Campaign Management| We have added a section <strong>"Bidding limits" </strong> in [Bidding](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1745292444424193) to clarify the verification mechanism for the bid price. To learn about the maximum bid price you can specify, see the new topic [Appendix-Bidding limits](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1750444779586561).

|November 11th, 2022|Doc enhancement |Campaign Management|We will deprecate the placements of BuzzVideo and Babe (`PLACEMENT_TOPBUZZ`) in late November, 2022. This will not impact your existing ads. |November 11th, 2022|Doc enhancement |Campaign Management|We have added a note to the descriptions of `placement_type` and `placements` in [/adgroup/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739499616346114) that these two parameters cannot be updated after the ad group has been created.|
|November 4th, 2022| Product enhancement|Creative Management|We have added an enum value `DOWNLOAD_CARD` for `creative_portfolio_type` and several related fields in [/creative/portfolio/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739091950439426) and [/creative/portfolio/get/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739092113671170) so that you can include a Download Card in your creative portfolio.|
|November 4th, 2022| Product enhancement|Campaign Management|We have fully released the optimization goal `ENGAGED_VIEW`. Allowlisting of this feature is no longer needed. See [Enumeration - Optimization Goal](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1737174886619138) for the supported optimization goals.  |
|November 4th, 2022| Product enhancement|Campaign Management|We have fully released the field `operation_status` for endpoints [/ad/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739953377508354), [/adgroup/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739499616346114), and [/campaign/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739318962329602). Allowlisting of this feature is no longer needed.  |
|November 4th, 2022| Doc enhancement|Business Center|We have added a note to [/bc/advertiser/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739939020318721) that the endpoint does not support creating multiple ad accounts simultaneously in one Business Center.|
|November 4th, 2022| Doc enhancement | Creative Management|We have added two sections on how to use Countdown Sticker and Download Card in your ads in [Portfolios](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739361803446273).|
|November 4th, 2022| Doc enhancement|Reporting|We have added a note to [Audience report](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1738864928947201), [Playable ad report](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1738864940608513), [DSA report](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1738864960144385), and [Reservation ads reports](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1738864971714562) that CHUNK mode only supports synchronous basic reports.|
```

For details about the new interest category names and IDs, see [Gaming-related interest category](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1738865051947010).|
| August 26th, 2022 |Product enhancement|Business Center| We now support business licenses in Brazil and Mexico. As a result, `license_no`is a required field when you use [/bc/advertiser/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739939020318721) or [/advertiser/update/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1739939050770434) to create or update ad accounts in Business Center, and your ad account is registered in the Chinese mainland, Hong Kong, or in countries Brazil and Mexico. |
| August 26th, 2022 |Doc enhancement| Generic| We have updated the return code article to include more return codes you may encounter when using the v1.3 endpoints. For details, see [Return codes](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1737172488964097). |
| August 26th, 2022 |Doc enhancement| Generic| We have added the Ultimate level rate limits for 14 special endpoints to the rate limit list. For details, see "Endpoint-specific rate limits" section of [Rate limits](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1740029171730433). |
| August 19th, 2022 |Product enhancement | Creative Management | Smart Fix is a feature that helps you identify and fix video issues, such as video size, resolution, background music, and length. For details, see [Smart Fix](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1741472523309058). <br>The related endpoints are [/file/video/ad/upload/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1737587322856449), [/video/fix/task/create/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1741468875279361) and [/video/fix/task/get/](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1741469487859714). |
| August 15th, 2022 | New API version | /| TikTok API for Business has been upgrated from v1.2 to v1.3. For details, see [Version 1.3](https://ads.tiktok.com/marketing_api/docs?id=1740579480076290). |
